When I run this 
```// Returns an array of all of the non-empty text nodes
function collectNonEmptyTextNodes(element) {
  let textElements = [];

  function recurseThroughNodes(node) {
    // If the node is a text node and its not empty push it onto the textElements array
    if (node.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE && node.textContent.trim() !== "") {
      textElements.push(node);
    }
    // If the node is an element node, check all of its children nodes for text
    else if (node.nodeType === Node.ELEMENT_NODE) {
      Array.from(node.childNodes).forEach(recurseThroughNodes);
    }
  }

  // Recursively go through every element
  recurseThroughNodes(element);

  // Return the array of non empty elements
  return textElements;
}

function boldEveryXWord(textNode, wordPercentage, boldXWords) {
  const fullText = textNode.textContent;
  const words = fullText.split(/\s+/);
  const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();

  words.forEach((word, i) => {
    if (i % boldXWords === 0) {
      const boldLength = Math.ceil(word.length * (wordPercentage / 100));
      const boldPart = word.substring(0, boldLength);
      const restPart = word.substring(boldLength);

      // Create bold element
      const boldEl = document.createElement("strong");
      boldEl.textContent = boldPart;
      fragment.appendChild(boldEl);

      // Append the rest part of the word
      const restTextNode = document.createTextNode(restPart + " ");
      fragment.appendChild(restTextNode);
    } else {
      const textNode = document.createTextNode(word + " ");
      fragment.appendChild(textNode);
    }
  });

  if (textNode.parentNode) {
    textNode.parentNode.replaceChild(fragment, textNode);
  }
}

function enableBionicReading(wordPercentage, boldXWords) {
  let elements = collectNonEmptyTextNodes(document.body);

  elements.forEach((el) => {
    boldEveryXWord(el, wordPercentage, boldXWords);
  });
}

enableBionicReading(30, 2);```

On a wikipedia page it removes the box that some of the elments are in and kind of messes up the ui. Here is the before

</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Website</th><td class="infobox-data"><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://davidgoggins.com/">davidgoggins<wbr>.com</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>David Goggins</b> (born February 17, 1976) is an American retired <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy_SEAL" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Navy SEAL">United States Navy SEAL</a>. He is also an <a href="/wiki/Ultramarathon" title="Ultramarathon">ultramarathon</a> runner, <a href="/wiki/Ultra-distance_cyclist" class="mw-redirect" title="Ultra-distance cyclist">ultra-distance cyclist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Triathlete" class="mw-redirect" title="Triathlete">triathlete</a>, <a href="/wiki/Public_speaker" class="mw-redirect" title="Public speaker">public speaker</a>, author of two memoirs, and was inducted into the <a href="/wiki/International_Sports_Hall_of_Fame" title="International Sports Hall of Fame">International Sports Hall of Fame</a> for his achievements in <a href="/wiki/Sport" title="Sport">sport</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> Goggins was also awarded the <a href="/wiki/Veterans_of_Foreign_Wars" title="Veterans of Foreign Wars">VFW</a> <a href="/wiki/Pro-Americanism" title="Pro-Americanism">Americanism</a> <a href="/wiki/Award" title="Award">award</a> in 2018 <sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> for his service in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces" title="United States Armed Forces">United States Armed Forces</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> Goggins also published a <i><a href="/wiki/New_York_Times" class="mw-redirect" title="New York Times">New York Times</a></i> <a href="/wiki/New_York_Times_Best_Seller_list" class="mw-redirect" title="New York Times Best Seller list">Best Seller</a> book titled <i>Can't Hurt Me: Master Your Mind and Defy the Odds</i>.
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc">
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_and_education">Early life and education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Goggins&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1&amp;editintro=Template:BLP_editintro" title="Edit section: Early life and education"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Goggins was born on February 17, 1975, to Trunnis and Jackie Goggins. In 1981, he lived in <a href="/wiki/Williamsville,_New_York" title="Williamsville, New York">Williamsville, New York</a> on a street called Paradise Road with his parents and brother, Trunnis Jr.<sup id="cite_ref-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds-8">[8]</a></sup> While Goggins' neighborhood held "model citizens consisting of white people," he describes his home experience as "hell on Earth."<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-9">[9]</a></sup> Goggins' father owned the roller skating rink <i>Skateland,</i> located in <a href="/wiki/East_Buffalo_(New_York)" class="mw-redirect" title="East Buffalo (New York)">East Buffalo, New York</a>. At age six, Goggins often worked the night shift at Skateland alongside his family, organizing <a href="/wiki/Roller_skates" title="Roller skates">roller skates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds-8">[8]</a></sup>
Goggins’ mother left his father due to abuse and eventually moved herself and her children to live with Goggins' grandparents in <a href="/wiki/Brazil,_Indiana" title="Brazil, Indiana">Brazil, Indiana</a>.
</p><p>Goggins enrolled in second grade at a small <a href="/wiki/Catholic_school" title="Catholic school">Catholic school</a> and made <a href="/wiki/First_Communion" title="First Communion">First Communion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup> His brother, Trunnis Jr., returned to Buffalo to live with their father.<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-11">[11]</a></sup> When Goggins enrolled in the third grade, he was diagnosed with a learning disability due to the lack of schooling.<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-9">[9]</a></sup> He also found it difficult to learn as he was suffering from <a href="/wiki/Toxic_stress" class="mw-redirect" title="Toxic stress">toxic stress</a> because of the <a href="/wiki/Child_abuse" title="Child abuse">child abuse</a> that he suffered during his early years in Buffalo, New York. Because of the stress, he developed a <a href="/wiki/Stuttering" title="Stuttering">stutter</a>. Goggins explains how he was constantly in a <a href="/wiki/Fight-or-flight_response" title="Fight-or-flight response">fight-or-flight response</a> with <a href="/wiki/Social_anxiety_disorder" title="Social anxiety disorder">social anxiety</a> because of his stuttering.<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-9">[9]</a></sup> In school, Goggins was subjected to racism and the <a href="/wiki/Ku_Klux_Klan" title="Ku Klux Klan">Ku Klux Klan</a> held a local presence at the time in Brazil, Indiana.<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-9">[9]</a></sup> Goggins recalls he once found <i>"<a href="/wiki/Nigger" title="Nigger">Niger</a>  [</i><a href="/wiki/Sic" title="Sic">sic</a><i>] we're gonna kill you"</i> on his Spanish notebook. At 16, a student spray painted "<a href="/wiki/Nigger" title="Nigger">nigger</a>" on the door of Goggins' car.<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-11">[11]</a></sup>
</p><p>Before his freshman year, Goggins attended a pararescue jump orientation course. Goggins' grandfather had served in the Air Force before him and prompted him to attend.<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-11">[11]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career">Career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Goggins&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2&amp;editintro=Template:BLP_editintro" title="Edit section: Career"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Goggins applied to join the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force_Pararescue" title="United States Air Force Pararescue">United States Air Force Pararescue</a> and was accepted into training. During the training, he was diagnosed with <a href="/wiki/Sickle_cell_trait" title="Sickle cell trait">sickle cell trait</a> and was removed from training temporarily.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> He instead participated in <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force_Tactical_Air_Control_Party" title="United States Air Force Tactical Air Control Party">United States Air Force Tactical Air Control Party</a> (TACP) training and worked as a TACP from 1994 until 1999 alongside British counterparts Flt Sgt Jones, Flt Stg Nair and Pvt Noble,<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> when he left the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p><p>He later quit an exterminator job to become a Navy SEAL. He joined the reserves, eventually making the weight requirements to begin training as a SEAL after losing 106 lbs in three months. He graduated from <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy_SEAL_selection_and_training#Basic_Underwater_Demolition/SEAL_(BUD/S)_Training_(24_weeks)" title="United States Navy SEAL selection and training">BUD/S training</a> with BUD/S class 235 in 2001. Following SEAL Qualification Training (SQT) and the completion of a probationary period, he received the NEC 5326 as a Combatant Swimmer (SEAL) and was assigned to <a href="/wiki/SEAL_Team_5" class="mw-redirect" title="SEAL Team 5">SEAL Team 5</a>. In his 20-year military career, Goggins served tours in <a href="/wiki/Iraq_war" class="mw-redirect" title="Iraq war">Iraq</a> and <a href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" class="mw-redirect" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">Afghanistan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> In 2004, Goggins graduated from Army <a href="/wiki/Ranger_School" title="Ranger School">Ranger School</a>, and received the "Enlisted Honor Man" award, receiving a 100% peer evaluation.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-4">[4]</a></sup> Goggins was the 36th African-American Navy Seal in <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy_SEALs" title="United States Navy SEALs">United States Navy SEAL</a> history.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Charity">Charity</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Goggins&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3&amp;editintro=Template:BLP_editintro" title="Edit section: Charity"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After several of his military friends died in <a href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" class="mw-redirect" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">Afghanistan</a> in a 2005 helicopter crash during <a href="/wiki/Operation_Red_Wings" title="Operation Red Wings">Operation Red Wings</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-stripes.com_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-stripes.com-17">[17]</a></sup> Goggins began long-distance running to raise money for the <a href="/wiki/Special_Operations_Warrior_Foundation" title="Special Operations Warrior Foundation">Special Operations Warrior Foundation</a>, which gives college scholarships and grants to the children of fallen special operations soldiers.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> Competing in endurance challenges, including the <a href="/wiki/Badwater_Ultramarathon" title="Badwater Ultramarathon">Badwater Ultramarathon</a> three times, Goggins raised more than <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a>2 million for the Special Operations Warrior Foundation.<sup id="cite_ref-vfw.org_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vfw.org-19">[19]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marathon_and_ultramarathon_running">Marathon and ultramarathon running</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Goggins&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4&amp;editintro=Template:BLP_editintro" title="Edit section: Marathon and ultramarathon running"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In 2005, Goggins entered the San Diego One Day, a 24-hour ultramarathon in <a href="/wiki/San_Diego" title="San Diego">San Diego</a>. He then completed the <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas_Marathon" class="mw-redirect" title="Las Vegas Marathon">Las Vegas Marathon</a> in a time to qualify for the <a href="/wiki/Boston_Marathon" title="Boston Marathon">Boston Marathon</a>. In 2006, he entered the HURT 100 in Hawaii.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup> Goggins was invited to the 2006 Badwater-135, where he finished 5th overall.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2006, he competed in the Ultraman World Championships Triathlon in Hawaii, placing second in the three-day, 320-mile race. He also participated in the <a href="/wiki/Furnace_Creek_508" title="Furnace Creek 508">Furnace Creek-508</a> (2009).<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2007, Goggins placed third overall in the Badwater-135.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> He competed in the Badwater-135 in 2013 and finished 18th,<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> after a break from the event since 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2008, he was named a "Hero of Running" by <i><a href="/wiki/Runner%27s_World" title="Runner's World">Runner's World</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup> In 2016, Goggins won the Infinitus 88k in 12 hours. In the same year, he won the Music City Ultra 50k, and Strolling Jim 40 Miler.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> In 2020, Goggins ran the <a href="/wiki/Moab_240" title="Moab 240">Moab 240</a> ultramarathon, placing 2nd in the 241-mile event with a time of 63 hours and 21 minutes, approximately 95 minutes behind race winner <a href="/wiki/Michele_Graglia" title="Michele Graglia">Michele Graglia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p><p>Entrepreneur <a href="/wiki/Jesse_Itzler" title="Jesse Itzler">Jesse Itzler</a>, upon seeing Goggins perform at a 24-hour ultramarathon, hired Goggins to live with him in his house for a month. Itzler wrote about his experience on a blog and later published the story as a book <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1133582631">.mw-parser-output cite.citation{font-style:inherit;word-wrap:break-word}.mw-parser-output .citation q{quotes:"\"""\"""'""'"}.mw-parser-output .citation:target{background-color:rgba(0,127,255,0.133)}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-free a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-free a{background:url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/65/Lock-green.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-limited a,.mw-parser-output .id-lock-registration a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-limited a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-registration a{background:url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d6/Lock-gray-alt-2.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-subscription a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-subscription a{background:url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/aa/Lock-red-alt-2.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}.mw-parser-output .cs1-ws-icon .cs1-maint{display:none;color:#3a3;margin-left:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .cs1-format{font-size:95%}.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-left{padding-left:0.2em}.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-right{padding-right:0.2em}.mw-parser-output .citation .mw-selflink{font-weight:inherit}</style><cite class="citation book cs1"><i>Living With A SEAL</i>.</cite><span class="Z3988"></span><sup id="cite_ref-Living_with_a_SEAL_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Living_with_a_SEAL-30">[30]</a></sup>
</p><p>His <a href="/wiki/Self-help_book" title="Self-help book">self-help</a> memoir, <i>Can't Hurt Me: Master Your Mind and Defy the Odds</i>, was released on December 4, 2018. In the book he refers to the 40% rule, his belief that most people, even with considerable effort, only tap into 40% of their capabilities.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> A follow-up sequel <i>Never Finished: Unshackle Your Mind and Win the War Within</i> was published December 4, 2022.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Awards_and_decorations">Awards and decorations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Goggins&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5&amp;editintro=Template:BLP_editintro" title="Edit section: Awards and decorations"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table style="margin:1em auto; text-align:center;">
<tbody><tr>
<td colspan="3"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:United_States_Navy_Special_Warfare_insignia.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/United_States_Navy_Special_Warfare_insignia.png/200px-United_States_Navy_Special_Warfare_insignia.png" decoding="async" width="200" height="104" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/United_States_Navy_Special_Warfare_insignia.png/300px-United_States_Navy_Special_Warfare_insignia.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/United_States_Navy_Special_Warfare_insignia.png/400px-United_States_Navy_Special_Warfare_insignia.png 2x" data-file-width="587" data-file-height="305"></a></span>

<p><b><strong>Da</strong>vid Goggins </b><strong></strong> (born <strong>Feb</strong>ruary 17, <strong>19</strong>76) is <strong>a</strong>n American <strong>ret</strong>ired  <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy_SEAL" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Navy SEAL"><strong>Un</strong>ited States <strong>Na</strong>vy SEAL </a><strong>.</strong> He <strong>i</strong>s also <strong>a</strong>n  <a href="/wiki/Ultramarathon" title="Ultramarathon"><strong>ultr</strong>amarathon </a><strong></strong> runner, <strong></strong> <a href="/wiki/Ultra-distance_cyclist" class="mw-redirect" title="Ultra-distance cyclist"><strong>ultra</strong>-distance cyclist </a><strong>,</strong>  <a href="/wiki/Triathlete" class="mw-redirect" title="Triathlete"><strong>tri</strong>athlete </a><strong>,</strong>  <a href="/wiki/Public_speaker" class="mw-redirect" title="Public speaker"><strong>pu</strong>blic speaker </a><strong>,</strong> author <strong>o</strong>f two <strong>mem</strong>oirs, and <strong>w</strong>as inducted <strong>in</strong>to the <strong></strong> <a href="/wiki/International_Sports_Hall_of_Fame" title="International Sports Hall of Fame"><strong>Inte</strong>rnational Sports <strong>Ha</strong>ll of <strong>Fa</strong>me </a><strong></strong> for <strong>h</strong>is achievements <strong>i</strong>n  <a href="/wiki/Sport" title="Sport"><strong>sp</strong>ort </a><strong>.</strong> <sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><strong>[</strong>5] </a></sup><strong></strong> Goggins <strong>w</strong>as also <strong>awa</strong>rded the <strong></strong> <a href="/wiki/Veterans_of_Foreign_Wars" title="Veterans of Foreign Wars"><strong>V</strong>FW </a> <a href="/wiki/Pro-Americanism" title="Pro-Americanism"><strong>Amer</strong>icanism </a> <a href="/wiki/Award" title="Award"><strong>aw</strong>ard </a><strong></strong> in <strong>20</strong>18  <sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><strong>[</strong>6] </a></sup><strong></strong> for <strong>h</strong>is service <strong>i</strong>n the <strong></strong> <a href="/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces" title="United States Armed Forces"><strong>Un</strong>ited States <strong>Ar</strong>med Forces </a><strong>.</strong> <sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7"><strong>[</strong>7] </a></sup><strong></strong> Goggins <strong>al</strong>so published <strong>a</strong>  <i><a href="/wiki/New_York_Times" class="mw-redirect" title="New York Times"><strong>N</strong>ew York <strong>Ti</strong>mes </a></i> <a href="/wiki/New_York_Times_Best_Seller_list" class="mw-redirect" title="New York Times Best Seller list"><strong>Be</strong>st Seller </a><strong></strong> book <strong>ti</strong>tled  <i><strong>Ca</strong>n't Hurt <strong>M</strong>e: Master <strong>Yo</strong>ur Mind <strong>a</strong>nd Defy <strong>t</strong>he Odds </i><strong>.</strong>  </p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_and_education"><strong>Ea</strong>rly life <strong>a</strong>nd education </span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket"><strong>[</strong> </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Goggins&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1&amp;editintro=Template:BLP_editintro" title="Edit section: Early life and education"><span><strong>ed</strong>it </span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket"><strong>]</strong> </span></span></h2>
<p><strong>Gog</strong>gins was <strong>bo</strong>rn on <strong>Feb</strong>ruary 17, <strong>19</strong>75, to <strong>Tru</strong>nnis and <strong>Ja</strong>ckie Goggins. <strong>I</strong>n 1981, <strong>h</strong>e lived <strong>i</strong>n  <a href="/wiki/Williamsville,_New_York" title="Williamsville, New York"><strong>Willi</strong>amsville, New <strong>Yo</strong>rk </a><strong></strong> on <strong>a</strong> street <strong>ca</strong>lled Paradise <strong>Ro</strong>ad with <strong>h</strong>is parents <strong>a</strong>nd brother, <strong>Tru</strong>nnis Jr. <sup id="cite_ref-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds-8"><strong>[</strong>8] </a></sup><strong></strong> While <strong>Gog</strong>gins' neighborhood <strong>he</strong>ld "model <strong>cit</strong>izens consisting <strong>o</strong>f white <strong>peo</strong>ple," he <strong>des</strong>cribes his <strong>ho</strong>me experience <strong>a</strong>s "hell <strong>o</strong>n Earth." <sup id="cite_ref-auto2_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-9"><strong>[</strong>9] </a></sup><strong></strong> Goggins' <strong>fa</strong>ther owned <strong>t</strong>he roller <strong>ska</strong>ting rink <strong></strong> <i><strong>Ska</strong>teland, </i><strong></strong> located <strong>i</strong>n  <a href="/wiki/East_Buffalo_(New_York)" class="mw-redirect" title="East Buffalo (New York)"><strong>Ea</strong>st Buffalo, <strong>N</strong>ew York </a><strong>.</strong> At <strong>a</strong>ge six, <strong>Gog</strong>gins often <strong>wo</strong>rked the <strong>ni</strong>ght shift <strong>a</strong>t Skateland <strong>alo</strong>ngside his <strong>fam</strong>ily, organizing <strong></strong> <a href="/wiki/Roller_skates" title="Roller skates"><strong>ro</strong>ller skates </a><strong>.</strong> <sup id="cite_ref-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Goggins_Defies_the_Odds-8"><strong>[</strong>8] </a></sup><strong></strong> Goggins’ <strong>mo</strong>ther left <strong>h</strong>is father <strong>d</strong>ue to <strong>ab</strong>use and <strong>eve</strong>ntually moved <strong>her</strong>self and <strong>h</strong>er children <strong>t</strong>o live <strong>wi</strong>th Goggins' <strong>gran</strong>dparents in <strong></strong> <a href="/wiki/Brazil,_Indiana" title="Brazil, Indiana"><strong>Bra</strong>zil, Indiana </a><strong>.</strong>  </p><p><strong>Gog</strong>gins enrolled <strong>i</strong>n second <strong>gr</strong>ade at <strong>a</strong> small <strong></strong> <a href="/wiki/Catholic_school" title="Catholic school"><strong>Cat</strong>holic school <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career"><strong>Ca</strong>reer </span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket"><strong>[</strong> </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Goggins&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2&amp;editintro=Template:BLP_editintro" title="Edit section: Career"><span><strong>ed</strong>it </span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket"><strong>]</strong> </span></span></h2>
<p><strong>Gog</strong>gins applied <strong>t</strong>o join <strong>t</strong>he  <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force_Pararescue" title="United States Air Force Pararescue"><strong>Un</strong>ited
